The most recent monitoring results revealed that the lake's fish population has increased by 710,000 tons, reached 10.850,000 tons, a 40% increase compared to 2002, when the fish population was protected for the first time.
The Yellow River pink salmon is a rare species of salmon found in the Yellow River basin. It is an important component of the Yellow River basin ecosystem and has an important role in maintaining the diversity of the Yellow River basin ecosystem.
During the 20th century and the 1960s and 1970s, due to the large number of fish being caught and the decline of the population, the population of the lake's trout declined to 2,592 individuals in 2002.
In 2004, the Chinese Red List of Endangered Species listed the Yellow River pinkling as a critically endangered species.
From 2003, Qinghai province implemented a closure of the lake's salmon fishing, prohibition of all individuals, groups and individuals from fishing in the lake and its tributaries, prohibition of the sale and sale of salmon and its products.

The first day of the 2012 Shanghai International Contemporary Art Exhibition took place on 11 December at the Shanghai International Contemporary Art Exhibition in Shanghai. 64 artists from China and other countries participated in the event.
The second dual year exhibition is organized by the S. T. P. D. R. I. R. Foundation and the Chinese UCCA Bardentown Contemporary Art Center, which is a joint effort. Chinese UCCA Bardentown Contemporary Art Center director Tong Tao is the art director of the exhibition.
According to the exhibition team, the main theme of the 2010- 2011 Double Year Exhibition is " climbing over the stone to cross the river " , which is a metaphor for the transformation of society and the economy during this period. This metaphor also reflects the social and cultural development of the Shan people at the time.
The second double year exhibition covers an area of more than 12,000 square meters and consists of six connected buildings with exhibition halls. presenting six single exhibitions, namely " touching the stone over the river " , " passing through the border of the world " , " the world's most beautiful new world " , " the essence of art and the spirit of art " , " the border of the world " and " the essence of art and the spirit of art " .
In particular, 27 pieces of works by artists from Saudi Arabia accounted for more than 40 percent of the total number of exhibited works, included paintings, sculptures, theatrical performances. 12 pieces of works by Chinese artists also attracted attention, included works that used recycled materials to recreate classic landscape paintings.
